# Native Migration Phase Status

Last updated: 2026-04-07

## Status Protocol
- `PHASE X STARTED`: phase execution is active.
- `PHASE X COMPLETE`: all phase gates are satisfied and recorded.
- Each completion entry includes evidence links.

## Phase 0 Gate Evidence
1. Architecture layout and native module boundaries are defined:
   - `docs/NATIVE_CLIENT_MIGRATION_PLAN.md`
   - `docs/project-structure.md`
2. Native module scaffolds exist:
   - `native-core/`
   - `native-bridge/`
   - `native-ui/`
3. Shared versioned schema contracts exist:
   - `schemas/native/command-envelope.v1.json`
   - `schemas/native/telemetry-event.v1.json`
4. Single motor authority is specified:
   - `motor::MotorRuntime` in migration plan.
5. Java compatibility-only migration direction is documented:
   - `AGENTS.md` native migration policy
   - `docs/project-structure.md` native migration layer note

## Phase 1 Progress Evidence
1. Native bridge daemon scaffold now has startup enforcement:
   - `native-bridge/src/bridge_service.cpp`
   - local-only bind rejection (`local_only_bind_required`)
   - token-required rejection (`missing_token`)
2. Contract-first command envelope validation is active before accept:
   - `native-bridge/src/command_envelope_validator.cpp`
   - `invalid_schema` and `unsupported_command_type` rejection paths
3. Optional verifier mode enforces replay/timestamp checks:
   - `replay_rejected_timestamp`
   - `replay_rejected_command_id`
4. Telemetry event emission exists for startup and ingest outcomes:
   - `native-bridge/src/telemetry_event.cpp`
5. Bridge CLI exposes Phase 1 controls:
   - `native-bridge/src/main.cpp`

## Phase 1 Completion Evidence
1. Build toolchain verification succeeded:
   - `cmake --version` -> `4.3.1`
   - `cmake -S native-bridge -B build/native-bridge`
   - `cmake --build build/native-bridge --config Release`
2. Startup policy enforcement smoke checks passed:
   - non-loopback bind rejects with exit code `2` (`local_only_bind_required`)
   - missing token rejects with exit code `3` (`missing_token`)
3. Contract and verifier smoke checks passed:
   - accepted command path,
   - `invalid_schema`,
   - `unsupported_command_type`,
   - `replay_rejected_command_id`,
   - `replay_rejected_timestamp`
4. Telemetry evidence captured in:
   - `runtime/bridge/telemetry.ndjson`

## Phase 4 Completion Evidence
1. Native state ingestion boundary and contract added:
   - `native-core/include/xptool/core/state_frame.hpp`
   - `native-core/include/xptool/core/state_acquisition_service.hpp`
2. State acquisition hardening implemented:
   - `native-core/src/state/state_acquisition_service.cpp`
   - schema-version checks (`1.0`/`1.1`)
   - sequence regression rejection
   - deferred last-known-good recovery budget
   - terminal rejection after budget exhaustion
3. Runtime integration added:
   - `native-core/src/runtime_core/runtime_runner.cpp`
   - `tick_frame(...)` path emits `state_acquisition` telemetry
4. Acquisition smoke harness added and verified:
   - `native-core/src/state/state_acquisition_smoke_main.cpp`
   - `build/native-core/Release/xptool_native_core_state_acquisition_smoke.exe`
5. Verified reason-code evidence from smoke run:
   - `state_acquired`
   - `state_acquired_legacy_alias`
   - `deferred_missing_logged_in`
   - `deferred_schema_version_unsupported`
   - terminal `schema_version_unsupported` rejection

   - enforced by `scripts/verify_java_shim_retirement_gates.py`
6. Phase 9.3 config-shim removal completed:
   - removed `provideConfig(...)` from `runelite-plugin/src/main/java/com/xptool/XPToolPlugin.java`
   - deleted `runelite-plugin/src/main/java/com/xptool/XPToolConfig.java`
   - updated `scripts/verify_java_shim_retirement_gates.py` to enforce no `XPToolConfig` file and no plugin config-provider wiring
7. Phase 9.4 plugin-shim removal completed:
   - deleted `runelite-plugin/src/main/java/com/xptool/XPToolPlugin.java`
   - cleared plugin registration in `runelite-plugin/src/main/resources/runelite-plugin.properties` (`plugins=`)
   - updated `scripts/verify_java_shim_retirement_gates.py` to enforce no plugin/config shim files and no plugin registration entry
8. Phase 9.5 full gate pack completed:
   - `.\gradlew.bat compileJava` (`runelite-plugin/`)
   - `python scripts/verify_java_shim_retirement_gates.py`
   - `python scripts/verify_java_runtime_ownership_blocked.py`
